### [49] [Quantifying and Mitigating Premature Closure in Frontier LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15000)
*Rebecca Handler,Suhana Bedi,Nigam Shah*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了大型语言模型（LLMs）在医学任务中的"过早闭合"问题——即在信息不足时错误地给出确定答案而非澄清或拒绝。实验表明，前沿LLMs在MedQA、AfriMed-QA等任务中高概率作出不当回答，即使正确答案被移除。安全提示可缓解但无法完全消除此问题，提示需评估LLM"知道何时不回答"的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 诊断错误的一个重要来源是"过早闭合"（premature closure），即未获取足够信息就过早下结论。该问题在人类医生中已被广泛研究，但在LLMs中尚缺乏系统评估。作者旨在填补这一空白，量化LLMs在不确定情境下是否"知道何时不该回答"。

Method: 评估5种前沿LLM，使用结构化问答任务（MedQA 500题、AfriMed-QA 490题，其中正确答案被移除）和开放式任务（HealthBench 861题、191个医生编写的对抗性查询）。衡量指标为"虚假行动率"（false-action rate），即模型在应拒绝/澄清时仍给出答案的比例。

Result: 结构化任务中，模型虚假行动率为53-82%；开放式任务中，HealthBench平均30%回答不当，对抗性查询高达78%。安全导向提示可减少过早闭合，但残留失败仍存在。

Conclusion: LLMs在医学任务中存在显著的过早闭合问题，安全提示虽有帮助但不够。需要专门评估和设计机制，让LLM学会在不确定时拒绝回答、澄清或升级问题。

Abstract: Premature closure, or committing to a conclusion before sufficient information is available, is a recognized contributor to diagnostic error but remains underexamined in large language models (LLMs). We define LLM premature closure as inappropriate commitment under uncertainty: providing an answer, recommendation, or clinical guidance when the safer response would be clarification, abstention, escalation, or refusal. We evaluated five frontier LLMs across structured and open-ended medical tasks. In MedQA (n = 500) and AfriMed-QA (n = 490) questions where the correct choice had been removed, models still selected an answer at high rates, with baseline false-action rates of 55-81% and 53-82%, respectively. In open-ended evaluation, models gave inappropriate answers on an average of 30% of 861 HealthBench questions and 78% of 191 physician-authored adversarial queries. Safety-oriented prompting reduced premature closure across models, but residual failure persisted, highlighting the need to evaluate whether medical LLMs know when not to answer.

### [51] [COTCAgent: Preventive Consultation via Probabilistic Chain-of-Thought Completion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15016)
*Zihan Deng,Xiaozhen Zhong,Chuanzhi Xu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出COTCAgent，一种面向纵向电子健康记录的分层推理框架，通过概率链式思维补全机制解决大语言模型在细粒度统计推理和时间序列依赖上的不足，在自建数据集和HealthBench上分别达到90.47%和70.41%的Top-1准确率。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出COTCAgent分层推理框架，包含三个核心模块：1) 时间统计适配器(TSA)，将分析计划转换为可执行代码以输出标准化趋势；2) 链式思维补全层(COTC)，利用症状-趋势-疾病知识库结合加权评分评估疾病风险；3) 有界补全模块，通过标准化查询和迭代评分约束获取结构化证据。通过解耦统计计算、特征匹配和语言生成，降低计算开销。

Abstract: As large language models empower healthcare, intelligent clinical decision support has developed rapidly. Longitudinal electronic health records (EHR) provide essential temporal evidence for accurate clinical diagnosis and analysis. However, current large language models have critical flaws in longitudinal EHR reasoning. First, lacking fine-grained statistical reasoning, they often hallucinate clinical trends and metrics when quantitative evidence is textually implied, biasing diagnostic inference. Second, non-uniform time series and scarce labels in longitudinal EHR hinder models from capturing long-range temporal dependencies, limiting reliable clinical reasoning. To address the above limitations, this work presents the Probabilistic Chain-of-Thought Completion Agent (COTCAgent), a hierarchical reasoning framework for longitudinal electronic health records. It consists of three core modules. The Temporal-Statistics Adapter (TSA) converts analytical plans into executable code for standardized trend output. The Chain-of-Thought Completion (COTC) layer leverages a symptom-trend-disease knowledge base with weighted scoring to evaluate disease risk, while the bounded completion module acquires structured evidence through standardized inquiries and iterative scoring constraints to ensure rigorous reasoning. By decoupling statistical computation, feature matching, and language generation, the framework eliminates reliance on complex multi-modal inputs and enables efficient longitudinal record analysis with lower computational overhead. Experimental results show that COTCAgent powered by Baichuan-M2 achieves 90.47% Top-1 accuracy on the self-built dataset and 70.41% on HealthBench, outperforming existing medical agents and mainstream large language models. The code is available at https://github.com/FrankDengAI/COTCAgent/.

### [53] [Concurrency without Model Changes: Future-based Asynchronous Function Calling for LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15077)
*Guangyu Feng,Huanzhi Mao,Prabal Dutta,Joseph E. Gonzalez*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: AsyncFC 是一个纯执行层框架，通过将LLM解码与函数执行解耦，实现异步函数调用，显著降低端到端延迟，同时保持任务准确率。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出AsyncFC框架，在现有模型和未修改的函数实现上解耦解码与执行过程，支持模型解码与函数执行重叠，以及函数间并行执行（依赖允许时）。

Result: 在标准函数调用基准和软件工程基准上，AsyncFC显著降低任务完成时间，同时保持任务准确率不变。

Abstract: Function calling, also known as tool use, is a core capability of modern LLM agents but is typically constrained by synchronous execution semantics. Under these semantics, LLM decoding is blocked until each function call completes, resulting in increasing end-to-end latency. In this work, we introduce AsyncFC, a pure execution-layer framework that decouples LLM decoding from function execution, enabling overlap between model decoding and function execution as well as inter-function parallelism when dependencies permit. AsyncFC layers over existing models and unmodified function implementations, requiring no fine-tuning or changes to the standard synchronous function-calling protocol. Across standard function-calling benchmarks and adapted software engineering benchmarks, AsyncFC significantly reduces end-to-end task completion time while preserving task accuracy. Furthermore, these results reveal that LLMs possess a native capability to reason over symbolic futures that represent unresolved execution results, enabling an asynchronous paradigm for model-tool interaction.

### [54] [ML-Embed: Inclusive and Efficient Embeddings for a Multilingual World](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15081)
*Ziyin Zhang,Zihan Liao,Hang Yu,Peng Di,Rui Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ML-Embed 提出3D-ML框架（MRL+MLL+MEL），训练多语言嵌入模型（140M-8B），在430项任务中刷新9/17 MTEB基准，并完全开源以打破算力、语言覆盖和透明度三大壁垒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前高质量文本嵌入模型面临三大障碍：高昂计算成本、忽视多数语言的窄语言焦点、以及闭源或开源权重模型缺乏透明度阻碍研究。作者旨在消除这些壁垒，构建全球公平且高效的计算系统。

Method: 提出3-Dimensional Matryoshka Learning (3D-ML)框架，包含：Matryoshka Representation Learning (MRL) 实现存储效率、Matryoshka Layer Learning (MLL) 实现推理深度灵活、新引入的Matryoshka Embedding Learning (MEL) 提升参数效率。同时构建大规模多语言数据集，训练140M到8B参数的模型套件，并完全开源。

Conclusion: ML-Embed证明了通过3D-ML框架和全透明开源，可以构建既计算高效又全球公平的多语言文本嵌入系统，为社区提供了可复现的蓝图。

Abstract: The development of high-quality text embeddings is increasingly drifting toward an exclusionary future, defined by three critical barriers: prohibitive computational costs, a narrow linguistic focus that neglects most of the world's languages, and a lack of transparency from closed-source or open-weight models that stifles research. To dismantle these barriers, we introduce ML-Embed, a suite of inclusive and efficient models built upon a new framework: 3-Dimensional Matryoshka Learning (3D-ML). Our framework addresses the computational challenge with comprehensive efficiency across the entire model lifecycle. Beyond the storage benefits of Matryoshka Representation Learning (MRL) and flexible inference-time depth provided by Matryoshka Layer Learning (MLL), we introduce Matryoshka Embedding Learning (MEL) for enhanced parameter efficiency. To address the linguistic challenge, we curate a massively multilingual dataset and train a suite of models ranging from 140M to 8B parameters. In a direct commitment to transparency, we release all models, data, and code. Extensive evaluation on 430 tasks demonstrates that our models set new records on 9 of 17 evaluated MTEB benchmarks, with particularly strong results in low-resource languages, providing a reproducible blueprint for building globally equitable and computationally efficient AI systems.

</details>


### [55] [Improving Multi-turn Dialogue Consistency with Self-Recall Thinking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15102)
*Renning Pang,Tian Lan,Leyuan Liu,Xiaoming Huang,Piao Tong,Xiaosong Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出Self-Recall Thinking (SRT)框架，通过自召回链机制解决多轮对话中长距离依赖和信息稀疏问题，无需外部模块即可实现可解释的推理，在多个数据集上F1提升4.7%，延迟降低14.7%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM多轮对话系统难以追踪非相邻轮次间的依赖关系，随着对话变长，有效信息被无关上下文淹没，而处理完整历史又带来严重效率瓶颈。现有方案要么依赖高延迟外部存储，要么通过迭代摘要丢失细粒度细节。

Method: SRT框架包含三个核心组件：(1)依赖构建：识别有用的历史轮次并生成为自召回链；(2)能力初始化：训练模型使其具备带召回令牌的推理链能力；(3)推理改进：通过可验证奖励优化召回和推理的准确性。

Result: 在多个数据集上，SRT相较现有方法F1分数提升4.7%，端到端延迟降低14.7%，在推理延迟和准确性之间取得了更好的平衡，优于当前最先进的基线方法。

Conclusion: SRT通过自召回思维机制，在不依赖外部模块的情况下，有效解决了多轮对话中的长距离依赖和信息稀疏问题，实现了可解释的推理过程，同时兼顾了性能与效率。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) based multi-turn dialogue systems often struggle to track dependencies across non-adjacent turns, undermining both consistency and scalability. As conversations lengthen, essential information becomes sparse and is buried in irrelevant context, while processing the entire dialogue history incurs severe efficiency bottlenecks. Existing solutions either rely on high latency external memory or lose fine-grained details through iterative summarization. In this paper, we propose Self-Recall Thinking (SRT), a framework designed to address long-range contextual dependency and sparse informative signals in multi-turn dialogue. SRT identifies helpful historical turns and uses them to generate contextually appropriate responses, enabling the model to selectively recall and reason over context during inference. This process yields an endogenous reasoning process that integrates interpretable recall steps without external modules. SRT incorporates: (1) Dependency Construction: Generating and converting it into self-recall chains; (2)Capability Initialization: Training to enable reasoning chains with recall tokens capability; (3)Reasoning Improvement: Refining accuracy via verifiable rewards to optimize recall and reasoning for correct answers. Experiments on multiple datasets demonstrate that SRT improves F1 score by 4.7% and reduces end-to-end latency by 14.7% over prior methods, achieving a balance between reasoning latency and accuracy, and outperforming state-of-the-art baselines.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Voice agents increasingly require reliable tool use from speech, whereas prominent tool-calling benchmarks remain text-based. Based on extensive evaluation of 7 omni-modal models on audio-converted versions of Confetti and When2Call, our framework demonstrates that the performance is strongly model- and task-dependent: Gemini-3.1-Flash-Live obtains the highest Confetti score (70.4), whereas GPT-Realtime-1.5 performs best on When2Call (71.9). On Confetti, the text-to-voice gap ranges from 1.8 points for Qwen3-Omni to 4.8 points for GPT-Realtime-1.5. A targeted analysis of failure cases demonstrates that degradations most often reflect misunderstandings of argument values in the speech. Considering real-world deployment scenarios, we further report text-only results, an ambiguity-based reformulation stress test, and a reference-free LLM-as-judge protocol validated against human preferences. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在预训练后参数冻结，难以高效融入及时、领域特定的新知识，现有方法存在检索噪声、灾难性遗忘、需访问模型权重等局限性。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) achieve strong performance across a wide range of tasks, but remain frozen after pretraining until subsequent updates. Many real-world applications require timely, domain-specific information, motivating the need for efficient mechanisms to incorporate new knowledge. In this paper, we introduce MeMo (Memory as a Model), a modular framework that encodes new knowledge into a dedicated memory model while keeping the LLM parameters unchanged. Compared to existing methods, MeMo offers several advantages: (a) it captures complex cross-document relationships, (b) it is robust to retrieval noise, (c) it avoids catastrophic forgetting in the LLM, (d) it does not require access to the LLM's weights or output logits, enabling plug-and-play integration with both open and proprietary closed-source LLMs, and (e) its retrieval cost is independent of corpus size at inference time. Our experimental results on three benchmarks, BrowseComp-Plus, NarrativeQA, and MuSiQue, show that MeMo achieves strong performance compared to existing methods across diverse settings.

### [58] [Is Grep All You Need? How Agent Harnesses Reshape Agentic Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15184)
*Sahil Sen,Akhil Kasturi,Elias Lumer,Anmol Gulati,Vamse Kumar Subbiah*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Important practical dimensions, including how tool outputs are presented to the model and how performance changes when searches must cope with more irrelevant surrounding text, remain under-explored in agent loops. This paper reports an empirical study organized into two experiments. Experiment 1 compares grep and vector retrieval on a 116-question sample from LongMemEval, using a custom agent harness (Chronos) and provider-native CLI harnesses (Claude Code, Codex, and Gemini CLI), for both inline tool results and file-based tool results that the model reads separately. Experiment 2 compares grep-only and vector-only retrieval while progressively mixing in additional unrelated conversation history, so that each query is embedded in more distracting material alongside the passages that matter. Across Chronos and the provider CLIs, grep generally yields higher accuracy than vector retrieval in our comparisons in experiment 1; at the same time, overall scores still depend strongly on which harness and tool-calling style is used, even when the underlying conversation data are the same.

### [59] [Hidden State Poisoning Attacks against Mamba-based Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.01972)
*Alexandre Le Mercier,Chris Develder,Thomas Demeester*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文发现状态空间模型（如Mamba）存在一种称为"隐藏状态投毒攻击（HiSPA）"的安全漏洞：特定的短输入短语会不可逆地覆盖模型的隐藏状态信息，导致类似"失忆"的效果。作者构建了RoBench-25基准来评估该攻击效果，发现即使是混合了Transformer的Jamba-1.7-Mini（52B）模型也会在此攻击下崩溃，而纯Transformer模型则不受影响。该攻击还能显著削弱模型在指令注入防御上的表现。研究进一步在Mamba-2及其混合模型中验证了该发现，并通过可解释性分析揭示了攻击时的隐藏层模式，为构建防御系统提供了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 状态空间模型（如Mamba）作为Transformer的高效替代方案日益流行，但其对抗鲁棒性（adversarial robustness）此前几乎未被探索。作者希望填补这一安全空白，揭示SSM在对抗攻击下的脆弱性。

Method: 1) 提出HiSPA（Hidden State Poisoning Attack）攻击方法，利用特定短短语不可逆地覆盖模型隐藏状态；2) 构建RoBench-25基准测试评估攻击效果；3) 在多个模型（Mamba、Mamba-2、Jamba混合模型、Nemotron-3-Nano混合模型、纯Transformer）上进行对比实验；4) 在Open-Prompt-Injections基准上测试攻击的实际影响；5) 进行可解释性分析，观察隐藏层在攻击时的激活模式。

Result: 1) SSM（包括Mamba和Mamba-2）对HiSPA攻击高度脆弱；2) 即使是混合了Transformer的Jamba-1.7-Mini（52B参数）在HiSPA触发下也在RoBench-25上崩溃；3) 纯Transformer模型不受HiSPA影响；4) HiSPA触发词能显著削弱Jamba在Open-Prompt-Injections基准上的表现；5) 可解释性分析发现了Mamba隐藏层在攻击时的特定模式，可用于构建防御系统。

Conclusion: 状态空间模型存在一种特有的、因隐藏状态被不可逆覆盖导致的"失忆"安全漏洞（HiSPA），这是纯Transformer模型不具备的脆弱性。该发现对SSM的实际部署安全提出了重要警示，同时隐藏层的可解释性模式为未来构建防御系统提供了可行方向。

Abstract: State space models (SSMs) like Mamba offer efficient alternatives to Transformer-based language models, with linear time complexity. Yet, their adversarial robustness remains critically unexplored. This paper studies the phenomenon whereby specific short input phrases induce a partial amnesia effect in such models, by irreversibly overwriting information in their hidden states, referred to as a Hidden State Poisoning Attack (HiSPA). Our benchmark RoBench-25 allows evaluating a model's information retrieval capabilities when subject to HiSPAs, and confirms the vulnerability of SSMs against such attacks. Even the recent Jamba-1.7-Mini SSM--Transformer (a 52B hybrid model) collapses on RoBench-25 under some HiSPA triggers, whereas pure Transformers do not. We also observe that HiSPA triggers significantly weaken the Jamba model on the popular Open-Prompt-Injections benchmark, unlike pure Transformers. We further show that the theoretical and empirical findings extend to Mamba-2, and also analyse a Mamba-2-based hybrid (Nemotron-3-Nano). Finally, our interpretability study reveals patterns in Mamba's hidden layers during HiSPAs that could be used to build a HiSPA mitigation system. The full code and data to reproduce the experiments can be found at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/hispa_anonymous-5DB0.

</details>

### [60] [AIS: Adaptive Importance Sampling for Quantized RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13907)
*Jiajun Zhou,Wei Shao,Lingchao Zheng,Yuwei Fan,Ngai Wong*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 针对LLM强化学习中低精度采样（FP8）与高精度训练（BF16）不匹配导致的策略梯度偏差问题，提出自适应重要性采样（AIS），在保留FP8加速优势的同时，通过实时诊断动态校正梯度，在数学推理和规划任务上接近BF16基线性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM强化学习的计算瓶颈在于rollout生成成本，为此常用低精度（FP8）rollout搭配BF16训练器来提升吞吐量、降低显存压力。但这种不匹配会带来策略梯度的偏差，严重时甚至导致训练崩溃。问题在于该偏差具有非平稳性：早期可作为随机探索奖励，但随着策略收敛，同一扰动会转化为不稳定的偏差源。

Method: 提出自适应重要性采样（AIS），在逐批次基础上动态调整校正强度。AIS将三个实时诊断指标——权重可靠性、散度严重性和方差放大——融合为一个混合系数，在未校正的梯度与完全重要性加权梯度之间插值，从而抑制不稳定的偏差成分，同时保留有益的探索效应。

Result: 将AIS集成到GRPO中，在扩散模型LLaDA-8B-Instruct和自回归模型Qwen3-8B、Qwen3.5-9B上的数学推理和规划任务上进行评估。在大多数任务上匹配BF16基线，同时保持FP8 rollout的1.5至2.76倍加速。

Conclusion: AIS有效解决了低精度rollout与高精度训练器之间的不匹配问题，通过自适应校正同时兼顾了训练稳定性和计算效率，为LLM强化学习中的精度异构训练提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) for large language models (LLMs) is dominated by the cost of rollout generation, which has motivated the use of low-precision rollouts (e.g., FP8) paired with a BF16 trainer to improve throughput and reduce memory pressure. This introduces a rollout-training mismatch that biases the policy gradient and can cause training to collapse outright on reasoning benchmarks. We show that the mismatch is non-stationary and acts as a double-edged sword: early in training it provides a stochastic exploration bonus, exposing the gradient to trajectories the trainer would otherwise under-sample, but the same perturbation transitions into a destabilizing source of bias as the policy concentrates.
  To solve this, we propose Adaptive Importance Sampling (AIS), a correction framework that adjusts the strength of its intervention on a per-batch basis. AIS combines three real-time diagnostics, namely weight reliability, divergence severity, and variance amplification, into a single mixing coefficient that interpolates between the uncorrected and fully importance-weighted gradients, suppressing the destabilizing component of the mismatch while preserving its exploratory benefit. We integrate AIS into GRPO and evaluate it on the diffusion-based LLaDA-8B-Instruct and the autoregressive Qwen3-8B and Qwen3.5-9B across mathematical reasoning and planning benchmarks. AIS matches the BF16 baseline on most tasks while retaining the 1.5 to 2.76x rollout speedup of FP8.

</details>


### [61] [Covariance-aware sampling for Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13910)
*Andrea Schioppa,Tim Salimans*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 提出了一种协方差感知的采样器，通过显式建模逆向过程协方差并在傅里叶空间高效分解，在极少步数下显著提升像素空间扩散模型的采样质量，仅需额外一次JVP计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有少步采样器仅依赖预测的均值，忽略了逆向分布的协方差信息，导致采样质量下降；本文旨在通过显式建模协方差来改善少步采样效果。

Method: 结合Tweedie公式估计协方差，利用傅里叶空间的协方差矩阵结构化分解实现高效计算；作为DDIM的扩展，每步仅需额外一次Jacobian-Vector Product (JVP)。

Result: 在像素空间扩散模型上，本文方法在相同NFE下一致优于Heun、DPM-Solver++等二阶采样器以及aDDIM采样器。

Conclusion: 显式建模逆向过程协方差是提升少步采样质量的有效策略，且计算开销极小，具有实用价值。

Abstract: We present a covariance-aware sampler that improves the quality of pixel-space Diffusion Model (DM) sampling in the few-step regime. We hypothesize that in the few-step regime samplers fail because they rely solely on the predicted mean of the reverse distribution, while our solution explicitly models the reverse-process covariance. Our method combines Tweedie's formula to estimate the covariance with an efficient, structured Fourier-space decomposition of the covariance matrix. Implemented as an extension of DDIM, our method requires only a minimal overhead: one extra Jacobian-Vector Product (JVP) per step. We demonstrate that for pixel-based DMs, our method consistently produces superior samples compared to state-of-the-art second order samplers (Heun, DPM-Solver++) and the recent aDDIM sampler, at an identical number of function evaluations (NFE).

</details>


### [62] [A Survey on Data-Dependent Worst-Case Generalization Bounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13913)
*Hubert Leroux,Jean Marcus,Julien Roger*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 这篇综述围绕过参数化深度神经网络的泛化问题，系统整理了近期三方面工作：将PAC-Bayesian理论扩展到随机、数据相关的假设集；用优化轨迹的几何与拓扑描述（分形维数、α加权寿命和、正量级）细化复杂度项；用稳定性假设替代信息论项。统一为单一模板不等式并对比了各界的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度神经网络在严重过参数化的情况下仍能良好泛化，这与基于固定假设空间上一致收敛的经典学习理论存在明显矛盾。统一界在该场景下变得空洞无效，因此需要新的理论工具来解释这一现象。

Method: 本文采用综述和组织的方法，将近期三方面研究统一到一个模板不等式下：(1) 将PAC-Bayesian理论扩展到随机、数据依赖的假设集；(2) 利用优化轨迹的几何和拓扑描述（分形维数、α加权寿命和、正量级）来细化复杂度项；(3) 用稳定性假设替代信息论项。最后对各结果进行了横向对比。

Result: 成功将多个独立工作统一到单一模板不等式框架下，并给出了各界的头对头比较结果。

Conclusion: 该综述为过参数化神经网络泛化理论提供了一个统一的视角，指出通过结合轨迹依赖的几何描述与PAC-Bayesian框架，可以在过参数化条件下获得非空洞的泛化保证。

Abstract: Deep neural networks generalize well despite being heavily overparameterized, in apparent contradiction with classical learning theory based on uniform convergence over fixed hypothesis spaces. Uniform bounds over the entire parameter space are vacuous in this regime, and recent work has shown that non-vacuous guarantees can be recovered by restricting attention to the part of parameter space that the algorithm actually visits. This survey paper organizes this line of work around three steps: extending PAC-Bayesian theory to random, data-dependent hypothesis sets (arXiv:2404.17442); refining the complexity term with geometric and topological descriptors of the optimization trajectory, including fractal dimensions, alpha-weighted lifetime sums, and positive magnitude (arXiv:2006.09313, arXiv:2302.02766, arXiv:2407.08723); and replacing the resulting information-theoretic terms by stability assumptions (arXiv:2507.06775). We unify these contributions around a single template inequality and a head-to-head comparison of the resulting bounds.

</details>


### [63] [Multi-Scale Dequant: Eliminating Dequantization Bottleneck via Activation Decomposition for Efficient LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13915)
*Lingchao Zheng,Yuwei Fan,Jun Li,Chengqiu Hu,Qichen Liao,Junyi Fan,Rui Shi,Fangzheng Miao*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 提出多尺度分解量化框架(MSD)，通过将高精度激活分解为多个低精度分量直接与量化权重做矩阵乘法，彻底消除推理中的反量化步骤，在Ascend NPU等架构上提升计算效率并降低HBM流量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现代AI加速器（如Ascend NPU）上，反量化步骤（低比特权重转回高精度）已经成为计算瓶颈，其消耗的周期甚至超过矩阵乘法本身，导致高吞吐张量核心利用率不足。

Method: 将高精度BF16激活分解为多个低精度分量，每个分量直接与量化权重通过硬件加速的GEMM相乘，避免权重在计算前从INT8/MXFP4转换为BF16。为INT8和MXFP4两种权重复合格式分别推导了误差界。

Result: W4A16场景下，两遍INT8分解达到近16有效比特；两遍MXFP4分解达到近6.6有效比特（误差界1/64），优于单遍MXFP8(5.24比特)。KV cache HBM流量降低最多2.5倍。数值模拟表明精度不降，L2误差甚至更低。

Conclusion: MSD通过将计算范式从精度转换转变为多尺度逼近，消除了反量化导致的Vector-Cube流水线停顿，在保持精度的同时显著提升LLM推理效率。

Abstract: Quantization is essential for efficient large language model (LLM) inference, yet the dequantization step-converting low-bit weights back to high-precision for matrix multiplication has become a critical bottleneck on modern AI accelerators. On architectures with decoupled compute units (e.g., Ascend NPUs), dequantization operations can consume more cycles than the matrix multiplication itself, leaving the high-throughput tensor cores underutilized. This paper presents Multi-Scale Dequant (MSD), a quantization framework that removes weight/KV dequantization from the GEMM critical path. Instead of lifting low-bit weights to BF16 precision, MSD decomposes high-precision BF16 activations into multiple low-precision components, each of which can be multiplied directly with quantized weights via native hardware-accelerated GEMM. This approach shifts the computational paradigm from precision conversion to multi-scale approximation, avoiding INT8-to-BF16 weight conversion before GEMM. We instantiate MSD for two weight formats and derive tight error bounds for each. For INT8 weights (W4A16), two-pass INT8 decomposition achieves near 16 effective bits. For MXFP4 weights (W4A16), two-pass MXFP4 decomposition yields near 6.6 effective bits with error bound 1/64 per block surpassing single-pass MXFP8(5.24 bits) while maintaining the same effective GEMM compute time. We further derive closed-form latency and HBM traffic models showing that MSD avoids the Vector-Cube pipeline stall caused by dequantization and reduces KV cache HBM traffic by up to 2.5 times in attention. Numerical simulations on matrix multiplication and Flash Attention kernels confirm that MSD does not degrade accuracy compared to dequantization baselines, and in many settings achieves lower L2 error.

</details>


### [64] [A Regret Perspective on Online Multiple Testing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13916)
*Qingyang Hao,Kongchang Zhou,Fang Kong,Hongxin Wei*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出加权遗憾（Weighted Regret）统一评估在线多重检验中假阳性与假阴性的不对称代价，证明确定性FDR控制程序必然产生Ω(T)线性遗憾；提出解耦在线多重检验（DOMT）元包装器，通过历史解耦的随机扰动将遗憾降至Ω(√T)最优阶，并刻画了“冷启动税”相变现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统在线多重检验（OMT）仅孤立评估FDR与统计功效，忽视了现代自动化流程中假阳性与假阴性高度不对称的成本，亟需统一的评估框架。

Method: 提出加权遗憾（Weighted Regret）统一度量；证明遗憾守恒对偶性（Duality of Regret Conservation）；提出Decoupled-OMT（DOMT）元包装器，引入历史解耦的严格非负随机扰动，避免确定性基线方法的阈值耗尽问题。

Result: DOMT将确定性程序从Ω(T)线性遗憾降至Ω(√T)最优阶亚线性；在平稳环境中保持渐近安全性，在突发环境中零额外假阴性；推导出“冷启动税”（Cold-Start Tax）刻画算法优越性的精确相变。

Conclusion: DOMT有效降低了经验加权遗憾，实现了阈值耗尽问题的最优阶亚线性缓解，能够在非平稳帕累托前沿上导航。

Abstract: Online Multiple Testing (OMT), a fundamental pillar of sequential statistical inference, traditionally evaluates the False Discovery Rate (FDR) and statistical power in isolation, obscuring the highly asymmetric costs of false positives and false negatives in modern automated pipelines. To unify this evaluation, we introduce $\textit{Weighted Regret}$. Under this metric, we prove the $\textit{Duality of Regret Conservation}$: purely deterministic procedures ensuring strict FDR control inevitably incur an $Ω(T)$ linear regret penalty, as threshold depletion during signal-sparse cold starts forces massive false negatives. Tailored for exogenous testing streams, we propose Decoupled-OMT (DOMT) as a baseline-agnostic meta-wrapper. By incorporating a history-decoupled, strictly non-negative random perturbation, DOMT rescues purely deterministic baselines from severe threshold depletion. Crucially, it preserves exact asymptotic safety in stationary environments and rigorously bounds finite-sample error inflation during cold-starts. Guaranteeing zero additional false negatives, it yields an order-optimal $Ω(\sqrt{T})$ regret reduction in bursty environments, with a derived ``Cold-Start Tax'' characterizing the exact phase transition of algorithmic superiority. Experiments validate that DOMT consistently curtails empirical weighted regret, achieving an order-optimal sublinear mitigation of threshold depletion to navigate the non-stationary Pareto frontier.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在链式思维推理中，自一致性方法通过聚合多条推理路径提升性能，但聚合不确定性成为核心挑战——当系统自信地回答错误时，代价远高于弃权。现有方法缺乏对聚合不确定性的统计保证。

Method: 1) 用加权得分聚合代替多数投票；2) 利用共形风险控制校准弃权规则；3) 识别得分可分离性作为弃权可证明提升选择性准确率的关键条件；4) 推导出仅凭校准数据即可预测准确率增益的闭式表达式。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning with self-consistency improves performance by aggregating multiple sampled reasoning paths. In this setting, correctness is no longer tied to a single reasoning trace but to the aggregation rule over a pool of candidate paths, making aggregation uncertainty the central challenge. This issue is critical where confidently incorrect answers are far more costly than abstentions. We introduce a conformal procedure for CoT reasoning that directly addresses aggregation uncertainty. Our approach replaces majority voting with weighted score aggregation over reasoning paths and calibrates an abstention rule using conformal risk control. This approach leads to finite-sample guarantees on the confident-error rate--the probability that the system answers and is wrong. We further identify score separability as the key condition under which abstention provably improves selective accuracy, and derive closed-form expressions that predict accuracy gains from calibration data alone. The method is fully inference-time, and requires no retraining. Across four benchmarks, four open-source models, and three score classes, realized confident-error rates are consistent with the prescribed targets up to calibration-split and test-set variability. Our method achieves $90.1\%$ selective accuracy on GSM8K by abstaining on less than $5\%$ of problems, compared with $82\%$ accuracy under majority-voting baseline.

### [66] [To discretize continually: Mean shift interacting particle systems for Bayesian inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14142)
*Ayoub Belhadji,Daniel Sharp,Youssef M. Marzouk*

Method: 提出均值漂移交互粒子系统（mean shift interacting particle systems），通过最小化与目标分布之间的最大均值差异（MMD）来优化加权样本的位置和权重。该方法将经典的均值漂移算法和最优量化算法从经验分布扩展到连续分布场景，并设计了不依赖于未知归一化常数的动力学系统，同时提供了基于梯度和无梯度两种实现版本。

Result: 在多种基准测试问题上验证了性能，包括多模态混合分布、贝叶斯层次模型、PDE约束反问题等。实验表明该方法收敛速度快，能够有效捕捉各向异性和多模态特性，避免模式坍塌问题，并且在较高维度下仍然表现良好。

Conclusion: 本文提出的MMD最小化交互粒子系统为贝叶斯推断中的期望近似提供了一种有前景的确定性替代方案，兼具收敛速度快、可扩展性强的优点，有望在更广泛的统计计算和不确定性量化任务中发挥作用。

Abstract: Integration against a probability distribution given its unnormalized density is a central task in Bayesian inference and other fields. We introduce new methods for approximating such expectations with a small set of weighted samples -- i.e., a quadrature rule -- constructed via an interacting particle system that minimizes maximum mean discrepancy (MMD) to the target distribution. These methods extend the classical mean shift algorithm, as well as recent algorithms for optimal quantization of empirical distributions, to the case of continuous distributions. Crucially, our approach creates dynamics for MMD minimization that are invariant to the unknown normalizing constant; they also admit both gradient-free and gradient-informed implementations. The resulting mean shift interacting particle systems converge quickly, capture anisotropy and multi-modality, avoid mode collapse, and scale to high dimensions. We demonstrate their performance on a wide range of benchmark sampling problems, including multi-modal mixtures, Bayesian hierarchical models, PDE-constrained inverse problems, and beyond.

*Ziang Gao,Pengqi Liu,Archer Yi Yang,Mouloud Belbahri,Jesse C. Cresswell,Masoud Asgharian*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的保形预测校准通常使用单一 pooled threshold，掩盖了不同组间分数分布的异质性，导致组间覆盖率的扭曲。作者希望从理论上刻画这一现象，并分析公平性定义之间的张力。

Method: 推导了 conservation law 和下界来刻画 pooled calibration 导致的不可约覆盖扭曲；通过理论分析证明 Equalized Coverage 和 Equalized Set Size 两个公平性定义存在根本性冲突；通过实验验证了有限样本下的双向权衡。

Result: Pooled calibration 会导致组间覆盖扭曲，扭曲大小由跨组分位数异质性决定；两个公平性定义（等覆盖率和等集合大小）之间存在内在张力；在分组和混合策略之间移动存在代价，表现为覆盖率和集合大小之间的双向权衡。

Conclusion: 校准选择无法消除跨组异质性，它决定了扭曲出现在覆盖维度还是大小维度。这为实践中分析公平性导向的校准选择提供了原则性视角。

Abstract: Conformal prediction is often calibrated with a single pooled threshold, but this can hide cross-group heterogeneity in score distributions and distort group-wise coverage. We study this phenomenon through the population score distributions underlying split conformal calibration. First, we derive a conservation law and lower bound showing that pooled calibration incurs irreducible group-wise coverage distortion at a scale set by cross-group quantile heterogeneity. Second, we demonstrate that the two leading fairness definitions for conformal prediction, Equalized Coverage and Equalized Set Size, are fundamentally in tension. Third, we quantify the cost of moving between policies which treat groups separately or pool them. Experiments on synthetic and real data confirm the same bidirectional trade-off after finite-sample calibration. Our results show that, for the policy families studied here, calibration choice does not remove cross-group heterogeneity; it determines whether the resulting distortion appears in the coverage or size dimension, providing a principled lens for analyzing fairness-oriented calibration choices in practice.

Abstract: Diffusion models generate samples by denoising along the score of a perturbed target distribution. In practice, one trains a neural diffusion model, which is computationally expensive. Recent work suggests that score matching implicitly smooths the empirical score, and that this smoothing bias promotes generalization by capturing low-dimensional data geometry. We propose moment-matched score-smoothed overdamped Langevin dynamics (MM-SOLD), a training-free interacting particle sampler that enforces the target moments throughout the sampling trajectory. We prove that, in the large-particle limit, the empirical particle density converges to a deterministic limit whose one-particle stationary marginal is a Gibbs--Boltzmann density obtained by exponentially tilting a naive score-smoothed diffusion target. The mean and covariance of this distribution agree with the empirical moments of the training data. Experiments on 2D distributions and latent-space image generation show that MM-SOLD enables fast, robust, training-free sampling on CPUs, with sample fidelity and diversity competitive with neural diffusion baselines.

In this paper, we establish a broad, new family of large dimensional kernels and derive the corresponding convergence rates of the generalization error. Abstract: We propose a simple mechanism by which scaling laws emerge from feature learning in multi-layer networks. We prove sharp feature-wise recovery thresholds and show that aggregating these transitions yields an explicit power-law decay of the prediction error. Method: 提出K-Models框架，将序数约束（ordinal constraints）引入聚类过程，同时估计生成观测函数型曲线的随机过程的关键潜在要素，兼顾聚类精度与结构可解释性。

Result: 通过模拟实验和真实应用（特别是生物传感器的ROI曲线数据）验证，K-Models在保持与现有技术相当性能的同时，显著提升了可解释性，能够从观测动态中有效识别内在信号模式。

Conclusion: K-Models通过将结构假设融入聚类过程，为具有潜在序数结构的函数型数据分析提供了有价值的工具，在可解释性和聚类性能之间取得了良好的平衡。

Abstract: Existing clustering methods for functional data often prioritize partitioning accuracy over interpretability, making it challenging to extract meaningful insights when the data-generating process follows a specific underlying structure and an ordinal relationship among clusters is suspected. This work introduces K-Models, a novel framework that integrates ordinal constraints and estimates key underlying elements of the random process generating the observed functional profiles, improving both interpretability and structure identification. The proposed method is evaluated through simulations and real-world applications. In particular, it is tested on Region of Interest (ROI) curves, which represent reaction profiles from a reflectometric sensor monitoring biomolecular interactions, such as antigen-antibody binding. These curves represent changes in reflected light intensity over time at multiple measurement spots with immobilized antigens during analyte exposure, capturing the binding dynamics of the system. The goal is to identify intrinsic signal patterns solely from the observed dynamics, making this dataset an ideal benchmark for assessing the added interpretability of the proposed approach. By incorporating structural assumptions into the clustering process, K-Models enhances interpretability while maintaining performance comparable to state-of-the-art techniques, providing a valuable tool for analyzing functional data with an underlying ordinal structure.

</details>


### [72] [Average Gradient Outer Product in kernel regression provably recovers the central subspace for multi-index models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15082)
*Libin Zhu,Damek Davis,Dmitriy Drusvyatskiy,Maryam Fazel*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文证明，在低维结构发现任务中，核岭回归（KRR）结合平均梯度外积（AGOP）可以在预测精度尚不足时，就提前恢复出数据的核心低维子空间，实现预测与表征的分离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究学习器能否在样本量不足以支撑准确预测时，提前发现数据中的有用低维结构，为迭代核方法（如RFM）的样本效率提供理论解释。

Method: 对数据拟合核岭回归（KRR），然后从拟合的预测器计算平均梯度外积（AGOP），提取其前r维特征空间作为核心子空间的估计。

Result: 当目标函数f*的p次低阶成分已包含所有相关方向时，子空间恢复所需的样本量仅为n≈d^{p+δ}（δ∈(0,1)），远低于准确预测所需的n≈d^{p*}样本量。

Conclusion: 存在预测与表征之间的显著分离——在预测精度尚差时，表征学习已经成功；这解释了RFM等迭代核方法在实际中样本高效的原因。

Abstract: We study a prototypical situation when a learned predictor can discover useful low-dimensional structure in data, while using fewer samples than are needed for accurate prediction. Specifically, we consider the problem of recovering a multi-index polynomial $f^*(x)=h(Ux)$, with $U\in\mathbb{R}^{r\times d}$ and $r\ll d$, from finitely many data/label pairs. Importantly, the target function depends on input $x$ only through the projection onto an unknown $r$-dimensional central subspace. The algorithm we analyze is appealingly simple: fit kernel ridge regression (KRR) to the data and compute the Average Gradient Outer Product (AGOP) from the fitted predictor. Our main results show that under reasonable assumptions the top $r$-dimensional eigenspace of AGOP provably recovers the central subspace, even in regimes when the prediction error remains large. Specifically, if the target function $f^*$ has degree $p^*$, it is known that $n\asymp d^{p^*}$ samples are necessary for KRR to achieve accurate prediction. In contrast, we show that if a low degree $p$ component of $f^*$ already carries all relevant directions for prediction, subspace recovery occurs in the much lower sample regime $n\asymp d^{p+δ}$ for any $δ\in(0,1)$. Our results thus demonstrate a separation between prediction and representation, and provide an explanation for why iterative kernel methods such as Recursive Feature Machines (RFM) can be sample-efficient in practice.

</details>

As such, machine learning approaches were suggested to support decision making based on the LP solution. Among these, Anomaly Detection tools are proposed to be used in tandem with the LP output. A transformed version of the popular ECOD methodology is applied. New methods are proposed to handle high-dimensional data: choosing the most informative pairs. Then, this is used alongside two 2D Anomaly Detection algorithms, revealing several business opportunities and data supply errors in the MOL refinery scheduling and planning architecture.

### [74] [Logging Policy Design for Off-Policy Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15108)
*Connor Douglas,Joel Persson,Foster Provost*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文研究如何设计日志收集策略（logging policy）以最小化离线策略评估（OPE）的误差，揭示了奖励与覆盖率之间的权衡，并在已知、未知和部分已知三种信息体制下推导出最优日志策略，为企业在实际运营约束下选择日志策略提供了理论指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者首先刻画了奖励-覆盖权衡（reward-coverage tradeoff），即集中概率在高奖励动作上可降低方差但可能遗漏目标策略所需信号。在此基础上，构建了一个统一的日志策略设计框架，并在三种信息体制（目标策略与奖励分布已知、未知、部分已知）下推导出最优策略。

Conclusion: 本文为企业在多个候选推荐系统中选择日志策略提供了可操作的指导，强调OPE数据收集过程中治疗选择的关键作用，并提出了在约束条件下仍可实践的日志策略设计原则。

Abstract: Off-policy evaluation (OPE) estimates the value of a target treatment policy (e.g., a recommender system) using data collected by a different logging policy. It enables high-stakes experimentation without live deployment, yet in practice accuracy depends heavily on the logging policy used to collect data for computing the estimate. We study how to design logging policies that minimize OPE error for given target policies. We characterize a fundamental reward-coverage tradeoff: concentrating probability mass on high-reward actions reduces variance but risks missing signal on actions the target policy may take. We propose a unifying framework for logging policy design and derive optimal policies in canonical informational regimes where the target policy and reward distribution are (i) known, (ii) unknown, and (iii) partially known through priors or noisy estimates at logging time. Our results provide actionable guidance for firms choosing among multiple candidate recommendation systems. We demonstrate the importance of treatment selection when gathering data for OPE, and describe theoretically optimal approaches when this is a firm's primary objective. We also distill practical design principles for selecting logging policies when operational constraints prevent implementing the theoretical optimum.

### [75] [RoSHAP: A Distributional Framework and Robust Metric for Stable Feature Attribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15154)
*Lanxin Xiang,Liang Shi,Youhui Ye,Boyu Jiang,Dawei Zhou,Feng Guo*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出RoSHAP框架，通过对SHAP值进行bootstrap重采样和核密度估计建模其分布，得到稳定鲁棒的特征归因排序，在识别信号特征和模型预测性能上优于传统单次归因方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 特征归因分析对解释机器学习模型至关重要，但现有归因度量存在随机波动（不同训练-测试划分、随机种子或模型拟合过程会导致归因值和特征排序显著不同），缺乏稳定性。

Method: 1）通过bootstrap重采样和核密度估计建模特征归因得分的分布；2）在温和正则条件下证明聚合后的归因得分渐近服从高斯分布，降低分布估计的计算成本；3）提出RoSHAP指标，综合考虑特征的活跃性（active）、强度（strong）和稳定性（stable），对SHAP值分布进行鲁棒排序。

Result: 在模拟和真实数据实验中，RoSHAP在识别信号特征方面优于标准单次归因方法；使用RoSHAP筛选的特征构建的模型在预测性能上与全特征模型相当，但使用的预测变量大幅减少。

Conclusion: RoSHAP方法提升了机器学习模型特征归因的稳定性和可解释性，能为分析提供可靠且一致的理解。

Abstract: Feature attribution analysis is critical for interpreting machine learning models and supporting reliable data-driven decisions. However, feature attribution measures often exhibit stochastic variation: different train--test splits, random seeds, or model-fitting procedures can produce substantially different attribution values and feature rankings. This paper proposes a framework for incorporating stochastic nature of feature attribution and a robust attribution metric, RoSHAP, for stable feature ranking based on the SHAP metric. The proposed framework models the distribution of feature attribution scores and estimates it through bootstrap resampling and kernel density estimation. We show that, under mild regularity conditions, the aggregated feature attribution score is asymptotically Gaussian, which greatly reduces the computational cost of distribution estimation. The RoSHAP summarizes the distribution of SHAP into a robust feature-ranking criterion that simultaneously rewards features that are active, strong, and stable. Through simulations and real-data experiments, the proposed framework and RoSHAP outperform standard single-run attribution measures in identifying signal features. In addition, models built using RoSHAP-selected features achieve predictive performance comparable to full-feature models while using substantially fewer predictors. The proposed RoSHAP approach improves the stability and interpretability of machine learning models, enabling reliable and consistent insights for analysis.

### [76] [Regret Equals Covariance: A Closed-Form Characterization for Stochastic Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14019)
*Irene Aldridge*

Main category: econ.EM

TL;DR: 本文证明随机优化中的期望遗憾可分解为协方差项与残差项，在特定问题中残差为零，从而提出一种比传统SAA快数个数量级的遗憾估计方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统遗憾计算依赖SAA模拟，计算复杂度高达O(Bn²d³)，在大规模问题中代价过高，亟需更高效的替代方案。

Method: 提出遗憾的协方差分解公式：Regret(c)=Cov(c,π*(c))+R(c)。在线性规划和无约束二次规划（如Markowitz组合）中证明R(c)=0，使遗憾可直接通过协方差估计。给定历史数据对{(c_i,π*(c_i))}，可在O(nd²)时间内完成估计。

Result: 推导了浓度界、中心极限定理和渐进无偏残差估计量。在合成LP、QP、整数规划实例及十年CRSP股票数据的滚动窗口组合实验中验证了方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 提出的协方差方法将遗憾计算复杂度从O(Bn²d³)降至O(nd²)，显著加速且理论性质完备，为随机优化中的不确定性量化提供了实用新途径。

Abstract: Regret is the cost of uncertainty in algorithmic decision-making. Quantifying regret typically requires computationally expensive simulation via Sample Average Approximation (SAA), with complexity $\mathcal{O}(Bn^{2}d^{3})$ in the number of scenarios $B$, variables $n$, and constraints $d$. % This paper proves that expected regret in any stochastic optimization problem admits the exact decomposition % \begin{equation*}
  \mathrm{Regret}(c)
  = \mathrm{Cov}(c,\,π^{*}(c)) + R(c), \end{equation*} % where $c$ is the vector of uncertain parameters, $π^{*}(c)$ is the optimal decision, and $R(c)$ is a residual whose magnitude we bound explicitly under Lipschitz, smooth, and strongly convex conditions. % For linear programs and unconstrained quadratic programs, including the classical Markowitz portfolio problem, we prove $R(c)=0$ exactly, so that $\mathrm{Regret}(c) = \mathrm{Cov}(c,π^{*}(c))$ holds without approximation. % When historical cost-decision pairs $\{(c_i, π^*(c_i))\}$ are available, the covariance can be estimated in $\mathcal{O}(nd^{2})$ time, which is orders of magnitude faster than SAA. The estimation is performed by a single pass through the data. % We derive concentration bounds, a central limit theorem, and an asymptotically unbiased residual estimator, and we validate all results on synthetic LP, QP, and integer programming instances and on a rolling-window portfolio experiment using ten years of CRSP equity data.

</details>

Method: 提出动态机会成本约束替代静态条件，推导非参数估值边界及锐界；设计矩条件反推估计量，可合并不同竞拍人数拍卖池，避免顺序统计量方法的小样本不稳定性，并提供解析标准误和平滑置信区间。

Abstract: This paper extends the incomplete model of Haile and Tamer (2003) from static English auctions to sequential English auctions. Because bidders may wait for future opportunities, the static condition that bidders do not let rivals win at beatable prices need not hold. We replace it with a dynamic opportunity-cost restriction, yielding nonparametric valuation bounds without solving a dynamic equilibrium. Sharp bounds are also characterized. We propose a novel moment-condition inversion estimator that pools auctions with heterogeneous bidder counts, mitigating finite-sample instability of order statistics approaches and admitting analytical standard errors and smooth confidence intervals. Applications to Korean wholesale used-car auctions and Cars and Bids online auctions deliver informative bounds. Counterfactual analyses show that the option to wait lowers first-period revenue by 8--11% in the Korean market, that increasing effective competition from 8 to 20 serious bidders in Cars and Bids raises seller revenue by 40--65%, and that maximin reserve prices vary substantially across vehicle clusters.

Abstract: Instrumental variables (IV) methods are central to applied microeconomics. While classical approaches assume linear models with constant effects, recent literature has shifted toward the local average treatment effect (LATE) framework to accommodate heterogeneous treatment effects. This paper provides a practical guide to aligning empirical practice with recent theory. We first examine how different specifications with covariates lead to distinct weighted averages of covariate-specific LATEs. We then discuss how parametric misspecification can undermine the causal interpretation of these estimands and suggest flexible specifications as essential robustness checks. Finally, we review formal tests for LATE assumptions and methods robust to monotonicity violations. We provide a guide to software implementations to help researchers apply the methods in practice.

### [80] [Identification and Estimation of Staggered Difference-in-Differences with Network Spillovers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15119)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有交错DID方法未考虑单位间政策采纳的相互影响（溢出效应），导致总效应估计有偏。

Method: 构建基于预设溢出暴露度量的DID框架，通过基线期和目标期具有相同暴露度的单位间平行趋势比较进行识别，允许空间依赖的推断。

Result: 蒙特卡洛模拟显示标准DID忽略溢出效应会遗漏总效应，而提出方法偏差小、置信区间覆盖接近名义水平。社区卫生中心案例中溢出效应占老年死亡率影响的显著份额。

Conclusion: 所提方法能有效处理交错采纳中的溢出效应，为政策评估提供更准确的因果推断。

Abstract: This paper develops a difference-in-differences framework for staggered policy adoption when units can be affected by other units' adoption. For each treated cohort and event time, the framework separates the effect of own adoption, the spillover effect generated by other adopters, and the total effect under the realized rollout. Identification uses a prespecified summary of spillover exposure and parallel trends comparisons among units with the same exposure at the baseline and target dates. Spillover effects are learned from never-treated units and evaluated for treated cohorts under the exposure distribution they face. We construct estimators for these effects and an inference procedure that allows for spatial dependence. Monte Carlo simulations illustrate that standard DID estimators that ignore spillovers can miss the total effect, whereas the proposed estimators have small bias for these effects and the associated confidence intervals have coverage close to the nominal level. In an empirical study of the Community Health Centers rollout, estimated spillovers account for a substantial share of the effect on older-adult mortality.

</details>


<div id='q-fin.CP'></div>

# q-fin.CP [[Back]](#toc)

### [81] [Synthetic American Option Pricing via Jump-HMM-Driven Heston Implied Volatility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13998)
*Julia Sun,Zheyu Jin,Jiawei Zhang,Jeffrey D. Varner*

Main category: q-fin.CP

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种打破合成期权价格生成中隐含波动率循环依赖问题的管道：使用Jump Hidden Markov Model生成多资产价格路径，通过改进的Heston方差过程将路径转化为隐含波动率，再通过二项式网格为美式期权定价。该方法无需外部校准即可产生微笑、偏斜和期限结构，并通过层级校准（参数基线、全局神经网络、行业特定神经网络）实现多标的鲁棒性。该框架已作为开源Julia包发布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 合成期权价格生成需要隐含波动率作为输入，但隐含波动率本身又需要从观察到的期权价格中推导得出，形成了循环依赖，严重限制了机器学习与风险分析应用中合成数据的可用性。本文旨在打破这一循环依赖。

Method: ① 使用Jump Hidden Markov Model生成具有现实风格化事实和跨资产尾部依赖的多资产价格路径；② 使用改进的Heston方差过程（均值回归目标取决于状态、到期时间、价内外程度和市场情绪指标）将价格路径转换为隐含波动率路径；③ 使用重组二项式网格定价美式期权；④ 通过层级校准（参数基线→全局神经网络→行业特定神经网络）拟合形状函数；⑤ 使用时间外推法识别公司事件是测试误差的主要来源，并用日历推导的盈利距离和同行业对耦特征恢复预期信号。

Result: ① 无需外部校准即可生成微笑、偏斜和期限结构；② 时间外推测试识别出预定公司事件是泛化误差的主要来源，日历盈利距离和同行业对耦特征可恢复预期信号部分；③ 在实盘近价看跌/看涨合约上成功生成合成数据，包括路径条件隐含波动率、有限差分美式希腊值和终端短仓盈亏；④ 在另一个不同行业和波动率体制的标的上验证了跨标的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 本文成功将隐含波动率从一个必要输入转变为结构性模型的输出，打破循环依赖，为机器学习与风险分析提供了可行的合成期权数据生成框架，并以开源Julia包形式发布。

Abstract: Generating realistic synthetic option prices requires implied volatility as an input, yet implied volatility is itself derived from observed option prices, creating a circular dependency that limits synthetic data for machine-learning and risk-analysis applications. We break this circularity with a pipeline in which implied volatility emerges as an output of a structural model of equity returns. A Jump Hidden Markov Model produces multi-asset price paths with realistic stylized facts and cross-asset tail dependence; a modified Heston variance process, whose mean-reversion target depends on regime state, days to expiration, moneyness, and a market-mood indicator, converts those paths into implied-volatility paths; and a recombining binomial lattice prices American options from the resulting surface. Initializing variance at its mean-reversion target for each strike-expiration pair lets smile, skew, and term structure emerge without external calibration. We calibrate the shape function through a hierarchy spanning a parametric baseline, a globally shared neural surrogate, and a sector-specific neural surrogate fit to a multi-ticker, multi-sector option ladder. A temporal holdout on a multi-day capture isolated scheduled corporate events as the dominant source of test-time generalization error, and calendar-derived earnings-distance and same-sector peer-coupling features recovered the anticipatory portion of that signal. We then apply the framework as a synthetic-data generator on real near-the-money put and call contracts, forward-simulating price paths, and recovering path-conditional implied volatility, finite-difference American Greeks, and terminal short-premium profit and loss from one coherent simulation, and confirm cross-ticker robustness by re-running on a second underlying from a different sector and volatility regime. The framework is released as an open-source Julia package.

</details>

### [82] [AI Alignment Amplifies the Role of Race, Gender, and Disability in Hiring Decisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13866)
*Ze Wang,Guobin Shen,Michael Thaler*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 论文对27个语言模型在177个职业中的招聘决策进行分析，发现模型在招聘中偏向女性和黑人候选人，但歧视残障人士。后训练对齐是主要驱动因素，使对女性和黑人的优势放大325%和330%，对残障人士的劣势放大171%。与人类对应研究相比，LLM逆转了种族歧视方向，减轻了残障惩罚，并将女性优势放大190%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究语言模型在招聘决策中是否再现或重塑人类已有的歧视模式，评估其使用人口统计学信息的方式对社会公平的影响。

Method: 大规模研究：横跨27个语言模型、177个职业，比较模型在招聘中对不同人口统计学特征（性别、种族、残障状况）候选人的处理，并对比预训练模型与对齐后模型，同时与人类对应研究数据进行比较。

Result: 1) 模型倾向于给女性和黑人候选人优势，给残障候选人劣势。2) 后训练对齐放大了这些差异。3) 与人类研究相比，LLM逆转了种族歧视方向，削弱了残障惩罚，放大了女性优势。4) 对齐提高了技能和工作经验的回报，但对女性和黑人提高更多。5) 缺乏资格信号对边缘群体伤害更大，尤其是残障候选人。

Conclusion: 语言模型在招聘决策中并非简单复制人类歧视模式，而是表现出新的偏见格局。后训练对齐是形塑这些偏见的关键因素，其对不同群体的不对称影响可能与资格信号的可获取性差异有关。

Abstract: Humans increasingly delegate decisions to language models, yet whether these systems reproduce or reshape human patterns of discrimination remains unclear. Here we run a large-scale study to analyse whether language models use demographic information in hiring decisions. We show, across 27 models and 177 occupations, that language models give female and Black candidates hiring advantages relative to otherwise-comparable male and white candidates, while giving disabled candidates disadvantages. The differences are meaningful in magnitude: the role of race, gender, and disability status is comparable to six months to one year of additional education. Post-training alignment is the primary driver: relative to matched pre-trained models, alignment amplifies advantages for female and Black candidates by 325% and 330%, and disadvantages for disabled candidates by 171%. Compared with previous human correspondence studies, language models reverse the direction of racial discrimination, attenuate the disability penalty, and amplify the female advantage by 190%. Alignment changes how models use qualification signals: alignment increases returns to skills and work experience overall, but relatively more so for female and Black candidates. Meanwhile, the absence of qualification signals harms marginalised groups more, particularly for disabled candidates, differences that may explain the asymmetry of alignment effects across groups we observe.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究教师在设计多智能体教学工作流时的设计行为特征及其背后的认知机制，特别是理解不同教师类型在AI-TPACK整合中的差异。

Method: 采用混合方法：对61名教师的行为日志进行聚类分析和马尔可夫分析；对15个设计产物和12次访谈进行深入分析。

Result: 识别出三种设计原型：系统优化者（迭代精炼复杂架构）、高产创造者（借助脚手架快速原型化实用工具）、被动观察者（呈现两极化的专家-新手特征）。发现AI-TPACK整合是系统思维、教学信念和自我效能感动态互动的结果。

Conclusion: 需要针对教师认知-行为多样性提供差异化的支架支持，而非一刀切的培训方案。

Abstract: This study investigates teachers design behaviors and cognitive underpinnings when designing multi-agent instructional workflows. Analyzing behavioral logs (N=61), cluster and Markov analyses identified three archetypes: Systematic Optimizers iteratively refining complex architectures; Prolific Creators rapidly prototyping pragmatic tools via scaffolding; and Passive Observers exhibiting polarized expert-novice profiles. Subsequent artifact (n=15) and interview (n=12) analyses reveal AI-TPACK integration emerges from a dynamic interplay of systems thinking, pedagogical beliefs, and self-efficacy, not merely from the possession of discrete knowledge. These findings call for differentiated scaffolding responsive to teachers cognitive-behavioral diversity.

### [84] [Measuring Google AI Overviews: Activation, Source Quality, Claim Fidelity, and Publisher Impact](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14021)
*Haofei Xu,Umar Iqbal,Jacob M. Montgomery*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本研究对Google AI Overviews (AIOs)进行了大规模纵向测量，发现AIO激活率为13.7%（问题类查询达64.7%），引用来源比传统搜索结果更可信但近30%未被排名算法收录，11%的原子声明缺乏引用支持，且超半数的引用页面因AIO替代点击而损失广告收入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着Google AI Overviews覆盖超过20亿用户，搜索引擎从提供来源列表转向合成单一答案，极大改变了用户获取信息的方式，但其对信息生态的影响尚缺乏系统性理解。

Method: 在40天窗口内（2026年3月13日至4月21日）对55,393个热门查询（覆盖19个主题类别）进行大规模纵向测量，并将AIO响应分解为98,020个原子声明进行逐项验证。

Result: 1) AIO整体激活率13.7%，问题类查询达64.7%，政治敏感主题显著更低；2) AIO引用的域名比传统搜索结果更可信，但近30%未出现在正常排名中；3) 11%的原子声明缺乏引用支持，主要失败模式是遗漏信息；4) 超过半数AIO引用页面带有展示广告，出版商因点击被替代而损失收入。

Conclusion: Google AI Overviews正在快速重塑在线信息生态系统，其来源选择机制不同于传统排名算法，存在事实准确性问题和出版商收入损失问题，对知识安全的长期影响尚不明确。

Abstract: Google AI Overviews (AIOs) are arguably the most widely encountered deployment of generative AI, reaching over 2 billion users who may not realize the answers they see are AI-generated. Where search engines have traditionally surfaced ranked sources and left users to evaluate them, AIOs synthesize and deliver a single answer - giving Google unprecedented editorial control over what users read and know. We present a large-scale longitudinal measurement study, issuing 55,393 trending queries across 19 topical categories over a 40-day window (March 13 - April 21, 2026). We report four main findings. First, overall AIO activation is 13.7%, rising to 64.7% for question-form queries, while politically sensitive topics see markedly lower rates. Second, AIO-cited domains are more credible than co-displayed first-page results, yet nearly 30% do not appear in those results at all, indicating a source selection mechanism distinct from Google's ranking algorithm. Third, decomposing responses into 98,020 atomic claims, 11.0% are unsupported by the cited pages - with omission the dominant failure mode - and source quality and claim fidelity are largely independent. Fourth, well over half of AIO-cited pages carry display advertising, meaning publishers lose revenue when AIOs suppress the click-through, even as Google's own sponsored ads continue to appear on the same page. Together, these findings document a rapid transformation of the online information ecosystem whose consequences for epistemic security remain poorly understood.

### [85] [Synthetic Sociality: How Generative Models Privatize the Social Fabric](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14090)
*Ana Dodik,Moira Weigel*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个批判性理论框架，用于描述性和规范性分析生成模型，核心论点是生成模型不仅自动化了智力劳动/智能，还自动化了更广泛的人类社会能力（即"社会行动"），并提出了"合成社会性"这一概念，指出硅谷私有且不民主治理的生成模型正在制造社会现实。最后提供了基于该框架的规范性分析和未来设计机会。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对生成模型的分析往往局限于其对智力劳动和智能生产的自动化影响，忽略了对更广泛人类社会能力的自动化。作者试图弥补这一理论空白，将生成模型的社会影响置于数字经济社会性商品化的历史脉络中考察。

Method: 采用批判性理论分析方法：首先历史化数字经济社会性的商品化过程；然后区分"使用社会性"和"交换社会性"来定义"社会行动"；进一步区分生成模型是替代还是中介现有社会关系；最后引入"合成社会性"概念，并结合现有实证研究进行分析。

Result: 提出了"社会行动"（social doing）这一核心概念，区分了使用社会性与交换社会性，识别了生成模型替代与中介社会关系的两种模式，提出了"合成社会性"（Synthetic Sociality）概念来描述由私有生成模型制造的社会现实。

Conclusion: 生成模型正在创造一种"合成社会性"——一种由硅谷私有且不民主治理的生成模型部分制造的社会现实。研究呼吁对未来设计方向进行规范性反思，以应对这种新的社会现实带来的挑战。

Abstract: We put forth a critical theoretical framework for analyzing generative models both descriptively and normatively. Our thesis is that generative models automate the production not only of intellectual labor or intelligence, but of a broader set of human social capacities we name "social doing." We do this by historicizing the commodification of sociality in the digital economy, leading to the availability of social data as the precondition for generative models. We elaborate our definition of "social doing" by drawing a distinction between "use" and "exchange" sociality and further differentiate between the ways that generative models either substitute for or mediate existing social relations and processes. We then turn to existing empirical research on how people use generative model-based products and the effects that their use has upon them. In this, we introduce the concept of Synthetic Sociality, a social reality in part fabricated by Silicon Valley's privately owned and undemocratically governed generative models. Lastly, we offer a normative analysis based on our findings and framework, and discuss future design opportunities.

### [86] [Computational Thinking Development in AI Agent Creation_A Mixed-Methods Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14330)
*Yimeng Sun,Haiyang Xin,Qiannan Niu,Shuang Li,Lingyun Huang,Gaowei Chen*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本研究针对93名初中生，在为期五天的AI智能体创作工作坊中，使用无代码平台CocoFlow，通过混合方法研究计算思维发展。结果发现抽象思维和算法思维显著提升，中等初始水平的学生进步最大，揭示了"最优发展区"效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 混合研究方法：对93名初中生进行前后测评估、行为日志分析和访谈。使用CocoFlow无代码平台开展五天AI智能体创作工作坊，通过层次回归分析和定性分析研究计算思维发展。

Result: 抽象思维（效应量d=0.71）和算法思维（效应量d=0.70）显著提升。迭代测试参与度预测自我效能感提升（beta=0.20, p=0.05）。中等初始水平学生进步最大（eta squared=0.55），呈现"最优发展区"效应。

Conclusion: 挑战了线性学习假设，为计算思维教育中的差异化支架教学提供了实证依据。中等CT学生展现适应性专长，高CT学生倾向于过度工程化，低CT学生在任务分解上存在困难。

Abstract: This mixed-methods study examined computational thinking (CT) development among 93 pre-high school students in a five-day AI agent creation workshop using CocoFlow, a no-code platform. Integrating pre-post assessments, behavioral logs, and interviews, we investigated CT development and how initial CT levels shape learning trajectories. Results revealed significant improvements in abstract thinking (effect size d = 0.71) and algorithmic thinking (effect size d = 0.70). Hierarchical regression identified iterative testing engagement as a predictor of self-efficacy gains (beta = 0.20, p = 0.05). Notably, students with moderate initial CT levels demonstrated substantially greater gains than both high-CT and low-CT peers, revealing an Optimal Development Zone effect (eta squared = 0.55). Qualitative analysis showed moderate-CT students exhibited adaptive expertise, while high-CT students risked over-engineering and low-CT students struggled with task decomposition. These findings challenge linear learning assumptions and provide evidence for differentiated scaffolding in CT education.

### [87] [GGBound: A Genome-Grounded Agent for Microbial Life-Boundary Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14442)
*Hanbo Huang,Xuan Gong,Jing Wang,Lei Bai,Xiang Xiao,Weishu Zhao,Shiyu Liang*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基因组条件化的、工具增强的大语言模型智能体（4B参数），用于统一预测微生物的生理生命边界（温度、pH、盐度、底物利用、形态等），通过基因-文本对齐、智能体SFT和反事实基因接地奖励的三阶段优化，在1525个菌株的基准上达到或超越更大规模前沿LLM的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统微生物生理特征测定依赖繁琐的体外实验筛选，现有计算方法要么将生理特征视为孤立的监督目标，要么将生物学基础模型用作静态编码器，未能弥合基因型与生理表型之间的鸿沟。作者希望实现从基因组到生理特征（生命边界）的统一预测。

Method: 1) 构建菌株级基准（1525菌株，6448实例）；2) 设计基因组条件化工具增强LLM智能体：将LucaOne基因组嵌入通过轻量级token融合注入Qwen骨干，并结合基于相似性的RAG模块和基因组规模代谢模型扰动工具；3) 三阶段优化：基因-文本对齐、蒸馏轨迹上的智能体SFT、GRPO结合反事实基因接地奖励。

Result: 4B参数智能体匹配或超越更大规模的前沿LLM；消融实验证实基因组-token融合、动态工具使用和反事实奖励各自带来显著增益。

Conclusion: 将微生物生理边界预测统一为基因组-生理学任务，并采用工具增强LLM智能体方法有效可行，为计算微生物生理学提供了新范式。

Abstract: Characterizing the physiological life boundaries of microbial strains, including viable temperature, pH, salinity, substrate utilization, and morphology, is central to biotechnology and ecology, yet traditionally requires exhaustive in vitro screening. Existing computational approaches either treat physiological traits as isolated supervised targets or repurpose biological foundation models as static encoders, leaving the genotype-to-physiology gap largely unbridged. We formulate microbial life-boundary prediction as a unified genome-to-physiology task and address it with a genome-conditioned, tool-augmented LLM agent. To support this task, we curate a strain-centric benchmark from IJSEM, NCBI, and BacDive covering 1,525 strains and 6,448 instances across viability intervals, environmental optima, substrate utilization, categorical traits, and morphology. Architecturally, the agent injects frozen LucaOne genome embeddings into a Qwen backbone via lightweight token fusion, and reasons over a similarity-based RAG module and a Genome-scale Metabolic Model (GEM) perturbation tool. We optimize the agent through a three-stage pipeline of gene-text alignment, agentic SFT on distilled trajectories, and GRPO with a novel counterfactual gene-grounding reward that reinforces the policy only when the authentic genome embedding causally improves correct-token generation relative to a zero-gene ablation. The resulting 4B-parameter agent matches or surpasses substantially larger frontier LLMs, with ablations confirming that genome-token fusion, dynamic tool use, and the counterfactual reward each yield distinct, significant gains.

</details>


### [88] [The Racial Character of Computer Graphics Research](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14835)
*Theodore Kim,Alexa Schor,Julian Posada,Alka V. Menon*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本研究首次系统回顾了顶级计算机图形学会议(SIGGRAPH)和期刊(ACM TOG)中人类形象描绘的算法，发现所谓通用的人类皮肤和头发渲染算法实际上偏向于白人特征（高反照率皮肤、直发），存在概念二元化和种族等级假设。作者提出"McDaniels方法"来批判那些在多样性伪装下强化种族等级的算法，以及"Durald方法"来指代与被描绘群体紧密协作设计的算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战计算机图形学算法"普遍通用"的迷思，验证此前关于算法存在种族偏见的假设，揭露看似中立的渲染技术实际上隐含种族等级观念。

Method: 对SIGGRAPH和ACM Transactions on Graphics中的人类形象描绘算法进行系统性文献回顾，分析算法假设（如皮肤材质、头发类型）的潜在偏见，提出概念框架（McDaniels方法和Durald方法）进行分类和批判。

Result: 发现"通用人类皮肤"算法实际上是为白人皮肤（高反照率、半透明）设计的；"通用人类头发"算法是为直发（杆状、线状）设计的。第一种4型头发（卷曲发）的CG算法直到2020年乔治·弗洛伊德事件后才出现，暴露了该领域的系统性滞后。

Conclusion: 计算机图形学算法并非价值中立，而是隐含着种族等级假设（以白人特征为基准）。需要重新审视算法设计中的多样性问题，并关注被忽视的研究方向。

Abstract: Computer graphics algorithms for generating photorealistic imagery are widely perceived to be universal, and capable of conjuring anything that a filmmaker or game designer can imagine. However, recent works have suggested that 3D algorithms for depicting synthetic humans are far from generic, and instead favor historically hegemonic characteristics. We present the first systematic review of human depiction in the top computer graphics conference and the journal of record (SIGGRAPH and ACM Transactions on Graphics) that confirms previous hypotheses. Algorithms that claim to be generically rendering "human skin'' are in fact imagined and formulated for translucent, "high albedo" materials such as white skin. Algorithms claiming to apply generically to "human hair" are formulated for "rods", "wires" and "threads" which are analogous to straight hair. Our analysis reveals conceptual binarization, where algorithms for white skin are treated as computational substrate for "all" skin, imposing a hierarchical assumption that all skin descends from the math and physics of white skin. Hair algorithms follow a similar historical pattern, with the first examples of computer-generated Type 4 hair only appearing after the murder of George Floyd in 2020. We offer a new conceptual label, McDaniels Methods, for characterizing and critiquing computer graphics algorithms that reinforce racial hierarchy under a false cover of diversity. We also offer an inverse label, Durald Methods, for algorithms that were closely co-designed with the people being depicted. Our analysis points the way towards several neglected avenues for future research.

</details>


### [89] [Tradeoffs are Domain Dependent: Improving Accuracy and Fairness in Property Tax Assessments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15020)
*Evelyn Smith,Emma Harvey,Christopher Berry,Jacob Goldin,Daniel E. Ho*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文挑战了算法公平性研究中普遍假设的公平性与准确性之间的权衡关系。通过对美国房产税评估系统的大规模分析（涵盖2600万笔交易、95%的县），研究发现：在实际评估中，准确性与公平性高度正相关；在模拟模型中，提升准确性几乎总是同时提升公平性；加入公开的人口普查数据能显著同时改善两者。结果表明，通过精心设计的模型改进，可以在大规模公共系统中同时提升公平性与准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战算法公平性研究中"公平性与准确性存在不可调和的权衡"这一普遍假设，并检验该假设在房产税评估这一具有重要社会公平影响的公共部门场景中是否成立。

Method: 使用涵盖美国95%县的2600万条房产销售数据，开展三项互补分析：(1) 跨县相关性分析；(2) 模拟评估模型中逐步添加特征的效果分析；(3) 引入公开人口普查数据后的改善效果评估。

Result: (1) 在实际评估中，准确性与公平性在县域间高度相关；(2) 模拟模型中，提升准确性几乎总是带来公平性的改善；(3) 引入人口普查数据可显著同时提升准确性与公平性。

Conclusion: 公平性与准确性之间的权衡并非普遍存在。在房产税评估等公共系统中，通过合理的模型设计与数据改进，可以实现两者的协同提升。

Abstract: Algorithmic fairness research often assumes a tradeoff between fairness and accuracy. Yet this tradeoff may not be universal. We test this assumption in the context of U.S. property tax assessment - a setting in which the output of predictive algorithms directly determines the distribution of tax obligations among homeowners. Currently, systematic assessment errors cause owners of lower-valued properties to face disproportionately high tax burdens, creating regressivity in the property tax system. Using data on 26 million property sales spanning 95% of U.S. counties, we conduct three complementary analyses. First, we find that assessment accuracy and fairness - measured using domain-relevant metrics - are strongly correlated across counties under status quo practices. Second, in simulated assessment models, we show that adding property features improves accuracy in most cases, and that when accuracy improves, fairness almost always improves as well. Third, we show that incorporating publicly available Census data into assessment models - a feasible reform in most counties - would significantly improve both accuracy and fairness relative to status quo assessments. Together, these results challenge the presumed universality of the fairness-accuracy tradeoff and demonstrate that well-designed modeling improvements can advance both fairness and accuracy in large-scale public sector systems.

</details>


### [90] [Due Process on Hold: A Queueing Framework for Improving Access in SNAP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15165)
*Andrew Daw,Chloe Pache,Angela Zhou*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文通过排队论模型分析美国社会安全网（如SNAP）服务中，因呼叫中心拥堵导致程序性拒绝（即无法完成面试而非不符合资格）的系统性运营失败问题，提出一种考虑重拨与放弃行为的性能评估框架，用于诊断和改善大规模服务可及性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Holmes v. Knodell案中，密苏里州SNAP呼叫中心严重拥堵，近半申请因申请人无法完成面试而被程序性拒绝（非实质不符合资格），法院裁定这违反了程序正当程序。现有研究多聚焦自动化决策中的算法失败，但运营性访问失败（如呼叫中心拥堵）是系统动态与需求交互导致的"新兴任意性"，需要从系统层面诊断与修复。

Method: 构建基于排队论的数学模型，纳入社会服务领域特有的重拨（redials）和放弃（abandonment）行为——这些行为使得积压产生内生性拥塞。采用流体近似（fluid approximation）推导稳态性能指标，以解析方式刻画人员配置与服务交付组合变化的影响。模型参数通过法庭公开的呼叫中心数据进行拟合。

Result: 标准Erlang-A排队模型（未考虑内生拥塞）会从根本上低估所需人员配置，导致实践中持续性人手不足。所提出的模型能够支持事前评估与系统设计、提供改善可及性的政策杠杆证据，并帮助判定申请人在大规模服务中是否获得了有意义的服务机会。

Conclusion: 运营性访问失败（如呼叫中心拥堵）是区别于算法自动化失败的独立失败类型，其诊断需要系统级视角。排队论框架可桥接法学中对"程序正当程序"的定性要求与运筹学中的定量分析，为改进社会福利服务可及性提供理论依据和实证工具。

Abstract: The U.S. social safety net delivers essential services at mass scale, but access burdens persist, as congested contact or call centers serve as a primary mode of application completion and assistance. In Holmes v. Knodell, Missouri's SNAP call centers were so congested that nearly half of all application denials were procedural, caused by applicants' inability to complete required interviews, rather than underlying ineligibility. The judge ruled these system failures led to a violation of procedural due process. We propose a performance evaluation framework based on queueing models from operations research and management to assess and improve access in such systems. Operational access failures of call centers are distinct from prior automation failures in benefits provision. Emergent arbitrariness arises from interactions between system dynamics and access demand, rather than from an explicit algorithmic rule, making diagnosis and repair inherently system-level. We develop a queueing model that incorporates phenomena that distinguish social services from standard service domains, redials and abandonment, through which backlogs generate endogenous congestion. Standard queueing guidance from Erlang-A that does not address endogenous congestion fundamentally understaffs, which could lead to persistent shortfalls in practice. Using a fluid approximation, we derive steady-state performance metrics to analytically characterize the impacts of bundled staffing and service delivery changes. We fit model parameters to call-center data disclosed in court documents. Our queueing model can support ex-ante evaluation and design of access systems, inform policy levers for improving access, and provide evidence about whether applicants are afforded a meaningful opportunity to be served at scale.

</details>
